###### Remark .2.

Note that our value for TCE\operatorname{TCE} does not correspond to the reported value (i.e., 2.2196152.219615) in Ignatieva and Landsman ([2019](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#bib.bib42 "Conditional tail risk measures for the skewed generalised hyperbolic family"), Table 4, Panel F, column GH), which implies that there is an implementation error in that paper.

##### A simple implementation of the method of moments estimator:

This part records the method of moments formulas used to estimate (Ï‚âˆ,Î²)(\varsigma\_{\infty},\,\beta) in CorollaryÂ [2.2](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#S2.Thmtheorem2 "Corollary 2.2. â€£ 2 The mathematical framework â€£ Wishart conditional tail risk measures: An analytic approach1footnote 11footnote 1We thank Katja Ignatieva for her useful suggestions and remarks. We also thank the participants at CICIRM 2024, Ningbo, China and IME 2024, Chicago, USA, for their remarks. The usual caveat applies."), the parameters of the limiting distribution of xtx\_{t} in the Bru ([1991](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#bib.bib85 "Wishart processes")) case (i.e., when Ï‰=Î²â€‹Ïƒ2\omega=\beta\sigma^{2}). See GouriÃ©roux et al. ([2009](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#bib.bib32 "The Wishart autoregressive process of multivariate stochastic volatility"), Section 5) and GouriÃ©roux and Lu ([2025](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#bib.bib2 "Partial observability of implied volatility matrices: Identification and covolatilities filtering"), Prop.Â 2 and Prop.Â 5) for derivations.

At the population level (with iâ‰ ji\neq j), the identities are

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Î²\displaystyle\beta | =2â€‹(ğ”¼â€‹[xiâ€‹i,âˆ])2Varâ¡[xiâ€‹i,âˆ],\displaystyle=\frac{2\,\big(\mathbb{E}[x\_{ii,\infty}]\big)^{2}}{\operatorname{Var}[x\_{ii,\infty}]}, |  | (63) |
|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Ï‚iâ€‹i,âˆ\displaystyle\varsigma\_{ii,\infty} | =Varâ¡[xiâ€‹i,âˆ]2â€‹ğ”¼â€‹[xiâ€‹i,âˆ],\displaystyle=\frac{\operatorname{Var}[x\_{ii,\infty}]}{2\,\mathbb{E}[x\_{ii,\infty}]}, |  | (64) |
|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Ï‚iâ€‹j,âˆ2\displaystyle\varsigma\_{ij,\infty}^{2} | =Covâ¡[xiâ€‹i,âˆ,xjâ€‹j,âˆ]2â€‹Î²,\displaystyle=\frac{\operatorname{Cov}[x\_{ii,\infty},x\_{jj,\infty}]}{2\beta}, |  | (65) |

where Î²\beta does not depend on the index ii. As result, there are several estimator for Î²\beta and for Ï‚iâ€‹j,âˆ2\varsigma\_{ij,\infty}^{2}.

GouriÃ©roux and Lu ([2025](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#bib.bib2 "Partial observability of implied volatility matrices: Identification and covolatilities filtering")) suggest the following estimation procedure. Let Î¼^i\widehat{\mu}\_{i}, Î·i2^\widehat{\eta\_{i}^{2}}, and Î³^iâ€‹j\widehat{\gamma}\_{ij} denote the sample mean of xiâ€‹i,tx\_{ii,t}, the sample variance of xiâ€‹i,tx\_{ii,t}, and the sample covariance of (xiâ€‹i,t,xjâ€‹j,t)(x\_{ii,t},x\_{jj,t}), respectively. The plug-in estimators are

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Î²^=2nâ€‹âˆ‘i=1n(Î¼^i)2Î·i2^,Ï‚iâ€‹i,âˆ^=Î·i2^2â€‹Î¼^i,Ï‚iâ€‹i,âˆ2^=Î³^iâ€‹j2â€‹Î²^.\widehat{\beta}=\frac{2}{n}\sum\_{i=1}^{n}\frac{(\widehat{\mu}\_{i})^{2}}{\widehat{\eta\_{i}^{2}}},\qquad\widehat{\varsigma\_{ii,\infty}}=\frac{\widehat{\eta\_{i}^{2}}}{2\,\widehat{\mu}\_{i}},\qquad\widehat{\varsigma\_{ii,\infty}^{2}}=\frac{\widehat{\gamma}\_{ij}}{2\widehat{\beta}}. |  | (66) |

Note that we also have

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | ğ”¼â€‹[xiâ€‹j,âˆ]=Î²â€‹Ï‚iâ€‹j,âˆ.\displaystyle\mathbb{E}[x\_{ij,\infty}]=\beta\varsigma\_{ij,\infty}. |  | (67) |

###### Remark .3.

Relative to GouriÃ©roux and Lu ([2025](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#bib.bib2 "Partial observability of implied volatility matrices: Identification and covolatilities filtering")), there is a missing factor of 22 in the formulas for Î²\beta, Ï‚iâ€‹i,âˆ\varsigma\_{ii,\infty} and Ï‚iâ€‹j,âˆ\varsigma\_{ij,\infty}. Further to this, the Ï‚iâ€‹j,âˆ\varsigma\_{ij,\infty} in GouriÃ©roux and Lu ([2025](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.06401v1#bib.bib2 "Partial observability of implied volatility matrices: Identification and covolatilities filtering"), Eq. (7)) is off by a factor of Î²\beta.
